What I like about this place is that the prices are really good as in really low, but the quality still stays high. I go to these places I feel like I am shopping at the best of the best but honestly it‚Äôs just how the store is and that‚Äôs what I love. Also another really cool thing is that you can buy stuff like canteens here and plastic water bottles that are reusable. My dog is like my child and because of this I am cancelling my wellness plan and taking her to a real vets office where I can actually have a relationship with the vet and get transparency of costs without having to pay a monthly premium. < Text>
Took my new 9 week old Golden Retriever puppy on 03/13/20 for her first check up/ 2nd shots. Dr. Renn at the Northridge Banfield, was the one to check her, asked her regular questions. My puppy had ONLY diarrhea and slept non stop for 2 days, didn‚Äôt really eat much or drink. I thought because of change of food and normal puppy behavior, I didn‚Äôt really think much of it. Anyways, Dr. gave her a parvo test and she was positive and she and the nurse explained what it was and how lots of dogs don‚Äôt make it, etc. They gave me the option to do inpatient treatment only but was not a guarantee that she would make it. Told me in a few days my puppy was going to get worse, just to wait it out and eventually she will pass away. Dr. Renn rushed out of the room when she said she was contaminated and didn‚Äôt return. The nurse did come back to check up on us and made a comment that the DR. didn‚Äôt want to euthanize my puppy that day because she was still up and alive, SMH!

I took my puppy home, I was devastated but didn‚Äôt want to give up. I started researching home remedies, gave her pedialyte just to keep her hydrated. She kept playing, eating, drinking, no vomit, but again ONLY diarrhea. On 03/16 I came home from work and diarrhea was still there but it had blood in it. I took her to VCA emergency and I was there for 4 hours but it was the best thing I did. They gave me outpatient treatment and HOPE. Throughout her treatment at home, not once did she show any other symptom of Parvo. Diarrhea cleared in 2 days. My Nala got cleared of Parvo already and in a few days will be getting her continuous round of shots. She is strong and has parents that didn‚Äôt give up on her.

I‚Äôm writing this review now because I needed to wait it out to make sure my baby made it. This is not a review to bash Bandfield or the DR. but this happened and it shouldn‚Äôt be left unknown. I hope to anyone reading this always gets a 2nd opinion if you can.</Text>

Extremely knowledgeable, patient, thorough, thoughtful, and highly professional - In a nutshell, this was my experience with Robert Mansour and his associates.

Contacting an attorney is nerve wracking enough (at least for me) and I‚Äôve had to deal with quite a few for various services. Contacting Rob‚Äôs office and setting up an appointment was the most seamless and, dare I say, ‚Äúenjoyable‚Äù call that I‚Äôve had to make in a while. She said that she would discuss with Robert when he was free and get back to me about setting up an appointment, which she did in less than 30 minutes.

During the call with Rob, he could not be easier to speak with yet still very direct-to-the-point. Rob let me know what he thought my concerns were and, once I confirmed that I agreed, he went through his recommended solutions/options. <time>1485817370703< /time>< text>
Had 2 front tires put on my old car. The next day I noticed high pitched oscillating screeching. Commonly associated with brake pads that have worn down to the indicator. And the oscillation indicating that the rotors are warped. I took the car back in politely explained the symptoms that I was experiencing. And right off the bat Will the manager started accusing me of accusing him of causing damage to my car. I promise this was not the case. I suspect that my pads are worn down I just wanted to know for sure. I have pads and rotors I have been sitting on for a while waiting to install. So if it turns out that the brake pads were worn. It would not have been a surprise to me nor would it have been a problem for me to replace them both myself. I can tell you that my brake rotors we're not warped prior to the tire install. Because I had already planned on replacing my pads and rotors myself it would not have been a huge deal if they warped my rotors. The reason for the one star rating is because when I asked will to just let me know what was going on with the brake inspection and to please make sure that the lug nuts are properly torque. He got super defensive and standoffish telling me that everything is hand torqued and started to become quite intense. I decided to ask for my keys back and stated that I will be taking my car and leaving. I feel that his conduct was unprofessional. And after reading some reviews here this place seems to have a history of not assuming responsibility.

I also want to add that Will was trying to feed me bull crap by saying that rotors do not Warp. I called The Bureau of Automotive Repair services you verify his bold statement. It turns out rotors can Warp. And one of the main contributing factors is improper torquing of the lug nuts. So my first and last experience at this location was being lied to and accused of being that guy. I was nothing but nice and polite prior to wills episode. I advise using Firestone over Works. They run a tighter ship there. And less mistakes are made.

I forgot to add as insignificant as it is. Will offered me a $10 discount on a set of tires. Which at the time I was grateful for. When it came time for check out I was overcharged $10. Which I did not notice until I got to the parking lot. After I noticed the overcharge I was instructed to call back when will was on the clock. And that he could take care of it. At the time I assumed it was an honest mistake. But after my recent experience I now find myself wondering. It's sad that it is so hard to find honest reputable work in this area.

*update. After some research it turns out that rotors cannot warp. They experience lateral run-out. Which is caused by buildup of rust between the Hub and the rotor or by improper torquing of the lug nuts leading to uneven wear. And since my rotors were not removed there should be no variation between the mating surface of the Hub and the rotor. Which only leaves improper torquing of the lug nuts. Which brings me back to my point. I brought the car in because I suspected that the wheel was improperly torqued.

This is not the kind of experience anybody should have to expect When taking their car to a "professional" shop although technically rotors do not Warp as I found out it is a common shorthand phrase to describe lateral run-out. I feel that instead of arguing semantics will should have just offered to take a look and report back the findings as well as making sure the lug nuts wet properly torque to spec.< /text>

< review>
I just returned from a wonderfully delicious lunch at Aji. Christine the owner greeted me warmly as did all of the staff whom I interacted with. My roll was so fresh and scrumptious. This is the first time I've ever been able to finish my roll on my own and it wasn't because it was too small. It was the perfect amount. Treat yourself to a great meal at recently opened Aji Sushi and Grill, where Boathouse Sushi had been for several years. I am already looking forward to my next visit!
I was so famished when that beautiful roll with fresh cran and tempura shrimp was placed in front of me that I didn't take the time to photograph it, next time I definitely will, a feast for the eyes as well as the palate.

< review>
Golden Koi did a great job of accommodating protocols during Covid. Everyone had to wear gloves when serving themselves.  I normally do not like going to buffets because the thought of people eating and kicking their fingers and going back for seconds and touching the serving spoon with locked fingers is a disgusting thought.  But because everyone had to use gloves to serve themselves,  this thought was diminished. The food was good and being a seafood eater, there were plenty of selections to choose from. I think the dessert table could have had more variety but I cant complain about the main dishes. I ate on a weekend and I'm not sure if the menu is the same for weekdays but I was definitely pleased with the selection. I would have given it 5 stars since they weren't lacking, but like I said I'm not an avid buffet goer so 4 is the most I would give for any buffet. Definitely worth the drive to head out to roseville. Wish they had one like this in Elk Grove.<//review>

UPDATE!  The Koi Buffet is now open again! It's all the same great food as before. I just can't see the negative reviews here, cause service is great and the place is clean. The food is all fresh if you get here at a reasonable time. Best time is when they open! Fresh food and nobody has picked over all the food yet!  I gotta go back for those wings and ribs!

Closed for now due to the virus thing, but I really can't wait till it opens again! This is the best buffet in the area for a reasonable price. It's under new management so it cleaner than before and the service is perfect. The food is a generous selection of Chinese foods that you don't normally see at most buffets.

What I really like are the fried chicken wings and the ribs! Yeah Chinese do the best Chicken and Ribs! They even have french fries here, just in case you don't want Chinese food. I've always found the food hot and fresh, but do go 1/2 hr before closing and expect all fresh food just for you, it won't happen. Go at opening 11am! I want this place to open again!</text>

< Review>
Pretty happy decision to eat there. Looked at the food before deciding and about 8/10 things looked pretty fresh. This was on a Thursday evening so maybe not the most busy time. At least not very busy when we were there. I imagine weekends to be busier.

This place is pretty big. Could seat many people if needed. Food was good and I think it's cool they have soft serve and regular ice cream.

Mostly pretty typical Asian buffet stuff with a few surprises. The Mei Fun was nice! Thin little rice noodles with a simple and warm flavor.

I might come back if I'm in the area and looking for a buffet again. Sushi wasn't great here but most non sushi buffets that offer it generally meet a low expectation for that.

Solid 4 stars. Service was friendly too! Maybe even more so than most buffets. I'll give them credit there.

5 stars if the sushi were better and more of the food items were fresh. But the price is quite good for what you're getting.

Maybe it's tough for buffets to compete at this price range though because Thunder Valley does a buffet that is bigger and about the same price for dinner on weekdays. Between the two, I'd have to give it to thunder but for the sake of variety I'd probably come here from time to time if I frequented this area a lot more.<//Review>

Not here, at ooen at least be smart when you go to a buffet, Golden Kois good is great to taste, fair priced, and they're always stocked, bot running low like some other chinese buffets. Maybe that's why they're one of only a few left around here?

From best potstickers I ever had ( because it tasted like they were partially deep fried) to their deep fries shrimp what else can i ask for?

Trust me theres more, just go!!!</text>

< text>
I am not sure why the others are saying the food isn't fresh and delicious.  It is every visit for me.  It must be the day and time of day I usually go (Sunday, about 1pm).  Everything is fresh and hot.  They couldn't restock crabs ü¶Ä fast enough. I enjoyed just about everything I normally would order at Chinese restaurants. I don't get food poisoning from eating there.

Three things I don't care for there: salad bar, sushi, and the grill to order meat. 1) Chinese food isn't about salad, it's about cook veggies. Don't eat that raw greens at buffet. 2) sushi is Japanese food. Chinese are notoriously bad at making sushi. If you ever had bad sushi, chances are the owner of that place is Chinese or Vietnamese.  3) I watch those guys grill...not sure what it is but they manage to burn the meat all the time. Plus they don't change tongs between raw and cooked meat. That's just asking for trouble. Avoid these 3 and you'll have a more enjoyable experience.

I dock a star for crappy service, as it is expected of Asian restaurants to have crappy service.</text>

< text>
Just yesterday my family had lunch at Golden Koi Buffet. This was the first and last time we visited this place. We didn't find any outstanding food in comparison to other buffets, but service turned out to be much worse. For more than an hour while we were eating our lunch nobody even tried to offer a refill or pick up durty plates from our table. We had to make a tower of dirty plates and left-overs in the middle of table. It seemed like they have forgotten about us or just ignored. We didn't even receive our meal ticket at the end, so strongly decided not to leave any tip for such shoddy service. But voila ... 10% tip (or as they call it service charge) was already included to our bill. Any attempts to get it waved were unsuccesfull. SO, KEEP IN MIND BEFORE YOU GO TO Golden Koi THAT YOU'LL BE CHARGED 10% MANDATORY TIP WHETHER OR NOT YOU RECEIVE ANY SERVICE.< /text>

<rate>1</rate>< Review>
Waiter was almost completely non-attentive. Never removed a single plate. I placed all used plated on a nearby table. We also had to request refills. Definitely could use some  coaching.

The cooks refilling the buffet were significantly more friendly and kept me updated on the ETA of what I was looking for.
They even looked me in the eyes as I was talking to them. I don't see a lot of that anymore.

I was going to give only a 2/5 star rating, but the cooks by themselves earned, and deserve, the third star.

- UPDATE -

Dropped to a 1/5 star. Prices are NOT posted. Adult dinner buffet is $16. Two children in our party, same age, charged different prices. Tip is added to the ticket. Our waiter didn't earn at time of anysize. I just had to wave him down to remove a stack of 4 plates. Total ticket for 2 adults, 2 children, and 2 softdrinks, and aadded tip... $51.04.

We will not be returning.< /Review>

< user_name>
BungleKitty< /user_name>
< review>
The service was wonderful, the people were very friendly, and were definitely on top of things. As for the food, it's mostly seafood oriented, so if you can't eat seafood or don't generally enjoy it, the number of items is severely limited. If you are a seafood buff, it looks very appetizing and I was very excited to see whole cooked crawfish among their selections, not something you generally see west of the Mississippi. I was also happy to see the bean-paste filled items, something my family greatly enjoys when we go to any oriental themed restaurant.
The soft serve ice cream, though, was definitely refreshing, having a vanilla custard flavor that was very delicious as opposed to the run-of-the-mill watered down vanilla you can find standard in a lot of other oriental buffets.
I would've been a lot happier, though, if there had been more beef-based products, or dishes that didn't have fattier-ended meats. The General Tso's chicken is also VERY Americanized, very sweet with very little spicy and sour. My current take-out place wins over The Golden Koi.<//review>
